Shorebird families include the sandpipers, plovers, oystercatchers, snipes, and stilts, among others. They are distinguished by their small-to-medium-sized, narrow, pointy bills, long legs, long pointy toes, long wings, and feeding behaviors. 		Photo: Red Knots feeding https://t.co/EvOIAwoQQJ
